calendars[0] = Calendar.setup({
inputField : 'FB_TXTB_TEXTBOX1_ERIK_0_ENT_10327_RI_3117_PK_-3',
trigger : 'F_FB_TXTB_TEXTBOX1_ERIK_0_ENT_10327_RI_3117_PK_-3',

selectionType : Calendar.SEL_SINGLE
});

showCalendar = function(index) {
  var indexInt = parseInt(index);
  var c = calendars[indexInt];
  if (c == null) return;
  c["configuring"] = 1;
  var inputField = document.getElementById(c.args["inputField"]);
  var isPeriod = inputField.getAttribute("class") == 'periodPicker';
  var curValue = inputField.value;
  c.selection.clear(false);
  if (curValue) {
    var hasTime = inputField.getAttribute("isTime");
    var monthFirst = c.args["dateFormat"].indexOf("%d") > c.args["dateFormat"].indexOf("%m");
    if (isPeriod) {
      var sepIndex = curValue.indexOf("-");
      var startD, endD;
      if (sepIndex >= 0) {
        var strStart = curValue.substring(0, sepIndex).trim();
        var strEnd = curValue.substring(sepIndex+1).trim();
        startD = Calendar.parseDate(strStart, monthFirst);
        endD = Calendar.parseDate(strEnd, monthFirst);
      }
      else
        startD = Calendar.parseDate(curValue, monthFirst);
      if (startD) {
        if (hasTime) c.setTime(startD.getHours() * 100+startD.getMinutes(), true);
        if (endD)
          c.selection.set([[Calendar.dateToInt(startD), Calendar.dateToInt(endD)]]);
        else
          c.selection.set([Calendar.dateToInt(startD)]);
      }
    }
    else {
      var dd = Calendar.parseDate(curValue, monthFirst);
      if (dd) {
        if (hasTime) c.setTime(dd.getHours() * 100+dd.getMinutes(), true);
        c.selection.set([Calendar.dateToInt(dd)]);
      }
    }
  }
  c.refresh();
  c["configuring"] = undefined;
}
